### Nos Imin ###

lineofimin1 = { # Head of the Minyar of Cuivienen
	name = Imin

	dynasty = dynasty_imin
	religion = faith_eldar
	culture = minyar

	sexuality = heterosexual

	trait = content
	trait = diligent
	trait = just

	# Base stats assigned through lotr_posthistory_effects because character dies during Years of the Trees
	diplomacy = 0
	martial = 0
	stewardship = 0 
	intrigue = 0
	learning = 0
	prowess = 0

	trait = education_learning_4
	trait = beauty_good_3
	trait = physique_good_3
	trait = twotreeslight
	trait = sailed_west

	2.1.1 = { #-4310.1.1
		birth = yes
	}

	2.2.1 = { #-4280.1.1
		add_spouse = lineofimin2
		set_relation_soulmate = character:lineofimin2
	}

	2.3.1 = { # TEMP DEATH
		death = { death_reason = death_sailed_west }
	}
}
